    this.parentElement.remove();
  };
  if (document.readyState === 'complete') {
    setTimeout(init, 100);
  } else {
    document.addEventListener('readystatechange', (event) => {
      if (event.target.readyState === 'complete') {
        setTimeout(init, 100);
      }
    });
  }"
